DECLARE @Stock_ID INT = 1;
DECLARE @Date DATE;
DECLARE @MaxAppearances TABLE (room_type_id INT, MaxAppearances INT, CurrentAppearances INT DEFAULT 0);
DECLARE @TotalRows INT = 1000, @CurrentTotalRows INT = 0, @DateRange INT = 14;
DECLARE @RoomType INT, @MaxForType INT, @CurrentForType INT, @Amount INT;
DECLARE @StartDate DATE = '2023-12-04', @EndDate DATE = '2023-12-17';

-- Populate the max appearances for each room type
INSERT INTO @MaxAppearances (room_type_id, MaxAppearances)
VALUES
(1, 7), (2, 13), (3, 11), (4, 9), (5, 12), (6, 10), (7, 11), (8, 9), (9, 5), (10, 9),
(11, 11), (12, 16), (13, 14), (14, 10), (15, 12), (16, 9), (17, 8), (18, 10), (19, 8), (20, 11),
(21, 8), (22, 6), (23, 6), (24, 14), (25, 13), (26, 10), (27, 13), (28, 12), (29, 8), (30, 9),
(31, 12), (32, 14), (33, 8), (34, 12), (35, 9), (36, 11), (37, 11), (38, 10), (39, 10), (40, 8),
(41, 6), (42, 15), (43, 6), (44, 9), (45, 5), (46, 10), (47, 13), (48, 8), (49, 8), (50, 13),
(51, 9), (52, 14), (53, 8), (54, 14), (55, 4), (56, 11), (57, 10), (58, 7), (59, 9), (60, 11),
(61, 10), (62, 13), (63, 11), (64, 8), (65, 14), (66, 11), (67, 8), (68, 17), (69, 9), (70, 6),
(71, 8), (72, 8), (73, 12), (74, 12), (75, 10), (76, 9), (77, 10), (78, 8), (79, 15), (80, 10),
(81, 11), (82, 13), (83, 12), (84, 8), (85, 10), (86, 9), (87, 8), (88, 16), (89, 9), (90, 9),
(91, 9), (92, 9), (93, 6), (94, 2), (95, 11), (96, 12), (97, 7), (98, 9), (99, 14), (100, 8);
-- ... [Your previous INSERT INTO @MaxAppearances code here] ...

-- Loop through each room type and insert or update rows
WHILE @CurrentTotalRows < @TotalRows
BEGIN
    DECLARE room_cursor CURSOR FOR
    SELECT room_type_id, MaxAppearances, CurrentAppearances FROM @MaxAppearances WHERE CurrentAppearances < MaxAppearances;

    OPEN room_cursor;
    FETCH NEXT FROM room_cursor INTO @RoomType, @MaxForType, @CurrentForType;

    WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
    BEGIN
        -- Generate a random date between @StartDate and @EndDate
        SET @Date = DATEADD(DAY, CAST(RAND() * @DateRange AS INT), @StartDate);

        -- Check if a row with the same date and room type already exists
        IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM [ckaram01].[Stock] WHERE [room_type_id] = @RoomType AND [Available Date] = @Date)
        BEGIN
            -- Update the amount for the existing row
            UPDATE [ckaram01].[Stock]
            SET [Amount] = [Amount] + 1
            WHERE [room_type_id] = @RoomType AND [Available Date] = @Date;
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            -- Insert a new row
            INSERT INTO [ckaram01].[Stock] ([Stock_ID], [Amount], [Available Date], [room_type_id])
            VALUES (@Stock_ID, 1, @Date, @RoomType);
           
            SET @Stock_ID = @Stock_ID + 1;
        END

        -- Update counters
        SET @CurrentTotalRows = @CurrentTotalRows + 1;
        UPDATE @MaxAppearances SET CurrentAppearances = CurrentAppearances + 1 WHERE room_type_id = @RoomType;

        -- Break if total rows reached
        IF @CurrentTotalRows >= @TotalRows
            BREAK;

        FETCH NEXT FROM room_cursor INTO @RoomType, @MaxForType, @CurrentForType;
    END

    CLOSE room_cursor;
    DEALLOCATE room_cursor;

    -- Break the outer loop if total rows reached
    IF @CurrentTotalRows >= @TotalRows
        BREAK;
END
